English

In the world of everyday life (a king sometimes uses his dependents and ornaments to serve the purposes of those who are dear to him like his sons, wives etc.)
and in the Vedas, it is declared that all the gods make their offerings to the devotee.
Even so, the Lord of Lakс╣гm─л uses sentient beings and non-sentient things to serve for ever
the purposes of those who have won His regard,
because He is independent and is their Master.
So, for us whose minds have been disciplined by the teaching of such as the prince of sannayasins (viz. ┼Ъr─л R─Бm─Бnuja),
the service of the Lord extends
as far as the service of those who are dear to Him (Bh─Бgavatas).

English

It may be asked,

What is the glory that the j─лva is capable of conferring on the Supreme Being?

With his body and the like, he can confer only such glory as non-sentient things do.
So this service is common to him and acit.
The special glory that he can be the cause of promoting must be by means of his intelligence or chaitanya.1

English

It has been said:

“Bhagav─Бn, who has all beings as His body,
rejoices when a j─лva does what is good
and does not rejoice when the action is evil.”

When a man acts in accordance with the ┼Ы─Бstras,
he gives thereby delight to the Lord
and thus does not let his generosity and other qualities run to waste,
but promotes the glory of the Lord
so that He extols him as in the words :-

“All these are, indeed, generous”.

pero promueve la gloria del Se├▒or
para que lo ensalte como en las palabras:-

“Todos estos son, de hecho, generosos”.

рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рдиреБрдЧреБрдгрдорд╛рдЧ рд╡рд░реНрддрд┐рдХреНрдХреБрдореНрдмреЛрджреБ тАШтАШрд╢реБрднреЗрддреНрд╡рд╕реМ рддреБрд╖реНрдпрддрд┐ рджреБрд╖реНрдХреГрддреЗ рддреБ рди рддреБрд╖реНрдпрддреЗрд╜рд╕реМ рдкрд░рдорд╢реНрд╢рд░реАрд░реАтАЩтАЩ(рднрд╛рд░рддрдореН рд╢рд╛рдиреНрддрд┐-рдкрд░реНрд╡ резрепреп-реирелред) рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рдпреАрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдйреБрдХреНрдХреБ рд╕рдиреНрддреЛрд╖рддреНрддреИ рдпреБрдгреНрдбрд╛рдХреНрдХрд┐ рдпрд╡рдйреБрдбреИрдп рдФрджрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдЧреБрдгрдЩреНрдЧрд│реН рдХреБрдорд░рд┐рд░рд╛рджрдмрдбрд┐ рдпрдореНрдореБрдЦрддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ тАШтАШрдЙрджрд╛рд░рд╛рд╕реНрд╕рд░реНрд╡ рдПрд╡реИрддреЗтАЩтАЩ(рдЧреАрддрд╛ рен-резрео) рдОрдйреНрд▒рд╡рдйреНрджрд╛рдйреЗ рдХреКрдгреНрдбрд╛рдбреБрдореНрдмрдбрд┐ рдпрддрд┐рд╢рдпрд╛рдзрд╛рдпрдХрдйрд╛рдореНред

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдЕрдкреН-рдкрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рдирд┐рддреНрдпрд░реБрдореН рдореБрдХреНрддрд░реБрдореН

(рдЖрд│рд╡рдиреНрджрд╛рд░реН-рд╕реНрддреЛрддреНрд░рдореН рекрем)

рддрдереИрд╡ рдирд┐рддреНрдпрд╛ рдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рд╢реН рдЪ рдИрд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд░рд╛рднрд┐рдкреНрд░рд╛рдпрдВ рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреН-рдХреГрддреНрдп
рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрдорд╛рдгреИрдГ рдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдпреИрдГ

тАЬрдкреНрд░рд╣рд░реНрд╖рдпрд┐рд╖реНрдпрд╛рдорд┐ рд╕-рдирд╛рде-рдЬреАрд╡рд┐рддрдГ”
(рдЖрд│рд╡рдиреНрджрд╛рд░реН-рд╕реНрддреЛрддреНрд░рдореН рекрем)

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЙрдХреНрдд-рд░реАрддреНрдпрд╛ рднреЛрдЧ-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рдореН рдЙрддреНрдкрд╛рджреНрдп рддрдиреН-рдореБрдЦреЗрдирд╛рддрд┐рд╢рдпрд╛рдзрд╛рдпрдХрд╛ рднрд╡рдиреНрддрд┐ ред

English

In the same way as the muktas (released souls) and the nityas (the s┼лris ) promote the glory of the Lord
by direct perception of the Lord’s will
and by acting in such a way as to give Him bhoga or enjoyment,

The prapannas, too, can give rise to a special kind of bhoga or enjoyment to the Lord
and thus promote His glory
as stated in the following ┼Ыloka :-

“When shall I always be Thy servant,
look upon Thee as my Master
and in this way give Thee delight?”.

Espa├▒ol

De la misma manera que los Muktas (almas liberadas) y los nityas (los s┼лris) promueven la gloria del Se├▒or
por percepci├│n directa de la voluntad del Se├▒or
y actuando de tal manera que le diera bhoga o disfrute,

Las Prapannas tambi├йn pueden dar lugar a un tipo especial de bhoga o disfrute del Se├▒or
y as├н promueve su gloria
como se indica en el siguiente ┼Ъloka:-

“┬┐Cu├бndo ser├й siempre Tu siervo,
Te mirar├й como mi Maestro
y de esta manera Te dar├й deleite?”

рдЕрдкреНрдкрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рдирд┐рддреНрдпрд░реБрдореН рдореБрдХреНрддрд░реБрдореАрд╢реНрд╡рд░рд╛рднрд┐рдкреНрд░рд╛рдпрддреНрддреИ рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреНрдХрд░рд┐рддреНрддреБрдкреНрдкрдгреНрдгреБрдЧрд┐рд▒ рдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдпрдЩреНрдЧрд│рд╛рд▓реЗ тАШтАШрдкреНрд░рд╣рд░реНрд╖рдпрд┐рд╖реНрдпрд╛рдорд┐ рд╕рдирд╛рдердЬреАрд╡рд┐рддрдГтАЩтАЩ(рдЖрд│рд╡рдиреНрджрд╛рд░реН рд╕реНрддреЛрддреНрд░рдореН рекрем) рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рднреЛрдЧрд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреНрддреИ рдЙрддреНрдкрд╛рджрд┐рддреНрддрдореНрдореБрдЧрддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ рдпрддрд┐рд╢рдпрд╛рдзрд╛рдпрдХрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реНрдЧрд│реНред

English

When the J─лva acts on any occasion consciously,
since his desired fruit, incidental though it be, has to come from the will of the lord,
the latter has to be ascertained from the ┼Ыastras
which disclose that the service rendered to His devotees is most delightful to him.

Espa├▒ol

Cuando el J─лva act├║a en cualquier ocasi├│n conscientemente,

(рдЧрд╛рд░реБрдб-рдкреБрд░рд╛рдгрдореН реирезреп-рем-реп)

English

“Devotion to me is of eight forms:
(1) love to my devotees without any thought of their faults;
(2) rejoicing at the adoration offered to me by another;
(3) delight in listening to stories concerning me;
(4) a change in the voice, in the eyes and in the body, while listening to such stories;
(5) trying to offer adoration to me;
(6) freedom from hypocrisy in one’s relations with me;
(7) meditation of me at all times;
(8) and not considering me as one from whom worldly benefits can be had -

if bhakti (which is of these eight forms) is found in a mleccha,
he should be respected as the best of Brahmins endowed with j├▒─Бna and bhakti;
he is a real sanny─Бsi, he is a wise man and he may be taught (the scriptures)
and from him one may learn the truth.
He is fit to be adored even like myself.”,

Espa├▒ol

“La devoci├│n para m├н es de ocho formas:
(1) Amor a mis devotos sin pensar en sus fallas;
(2) regocijarse en la adoraci├│n que me ofrece otra;
(3) Deleitarse en escuchar historias sobre m├н;
(4) un cambio en la voz, en los ojos y en el cuerpo, mientras escucha esas historias;
(5) tratando de ofrecerme adoraci├│n;
(6) libertad de hipocres├нa en las relaciones de uno conmigo;
(7) Meditaci├│n de m├н en todo momento;
(8) y no considerarme como uno de quien se pueden tener beneficios mundanos -

Si bhakti (que es de estas ocho formas) se encuentra en una mleccha,
Deber├нa ser respetado como el mejor de los brahmanes dotados de j├▒─Бna y bhakti;
Es un verdadero sanny─Бsi, es un hombre sabio y se le puede ense├▒ar (las Escrituras)
Y de ├йl uno puede aprender la verdad. Es apto para ser adorado incluso como yo “.

of all forms of service which a ┼Ыeс╣гa of the Lord may render,
that rendered to the Bh─Бgavatas is the most important
and is the most pleasing to the Lord,
in the same way as the fondling of the prince is most pleasing to the king.

es m├бs agradable para el rey.

English

Our being ┼Ыeс╣гas to Bh─Бgavatas arises from their being devotees to the Lord
and pertains to our essential nature.
It arises also from their qualities and knowledge,
which cause a desire in us to serve them,

(As Lakс╣гmaс╣Зa says) “I am his younger brother (by birth);
I have become his servant by his qualities”.

(That this relationship of being a ┼Ыeс╣гa is due both to our essential nature and to (our admiration for) their wisdom and character)
is also indicated (respectively) in the two phrases

  1. “bhaktas of the lord” and
  2. to “men like me”

(in the speech of N─Бrada quoted above).

Espa├▒ol

Nuestro ser ┼Ъeс╣гas a Bh─Бgavatas surge de sus devotos al Se├▒or
y pertenece a nuestra naturaleza esencial.
Surge tambi├йn de sus cualidades y conocimientos,
que causan un deseo en nosotros de servirles,

(Como dice Lakс╣гmaс╣Зa) “Soy su hermano menor (por nacimiento);
Me he convertido en su sirviente por sus cualidades “.

(Que esta relaci├│n de ser un ┼Ыeс╣гa se debe tanto a nuestra naturaleza esencial como a (nuestra admiraci├│n) por su sabidur├нa y car├бcter)
tambi├йn est├б indicado (respectivamente) en las dos frases

  1. “Bhaktas del Se├▒or” y
  2. a “hombres como yo”

(en el discurso de N─Бrada citado anteriormente).

English

Therefore it is the farthest limit of the service of the prapanna to perform,
as much as it lies in his power, service to the Bh─Бgavata,
since it is part of the duty of one who is ┼Ыeс╣гa to Bhagav─Бn.
So this outermost region of service to Bh─Бgavatas
should be kept properly cultivated
so that it may not become fallow land full of weeds.

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, es el l├нmite m├бs lejano del servicio de la Prapanna para realizar,
Por mucho que se encuentre en su poder, servicio al Bh─Бgavata,
ya que es parte del deber de alguien que es ┼Ъeс╣гa a Bhagav─Бn.
Entonces esta regi├│n de servicio m├бs externa a Bh─Бgavatas
debe mantenerse correctamente cultivado
de modo que no se convierta en tierra en barbecho, llena de malezas.

and

“Among the Lord’s retinue are two classes:
those that are dear to him and worthy of His trust
and those who are not.
To the former class belong the nityas, the muktas and the Bhagavat─Бs.
To the latter class belong Brahma and the other gods
who are subject to the sway of past karma.
The seeker after mukti should not adore the latter;”

As stated in the above following ┼Ыlokas in Pauс╣гkara samhita,
the devotee who is exclusively attached to the Lord
and whose dharma resembles that of a chaste wife

рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рд╕рдмрдиреНрдз-рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖-рдирд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдирддреНрд╡рд╛рджреН

It may be said to be adventitious also (due to up─Бdhi or conditions),
as it arises from a knowledge of one’s relationship to Bhagav─Бn.

Espa├▒ol

Se puede decir que es adventicio tambi├йn (debido a up─Бdhi o condiciones), como surge del conocimiento de la relaci├│n de uno con Bhagav─Бn.

If so, it may be asked,

“If both are Bh─Бgavatas,
would it not be inconsistent
that they should be both ┼Ыeс╣гa and ┼Ыesh─л to each other?”

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдкрд░рд╕реН-рдкрд░реЛрдкрдХрд╛рд░реНрдпреЛрдкрдХрд╛рд░рдХ-рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рджрд┐рдЧрд│рд┐рд▒реН рдкреЛрд▓реЗрдпреН
рдЗрдЩреНрдЧреБрдореН рд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзрдореН рдЗрд▓реНрд▓реИред +++(4)+++

рд╡рд┐рд╕реНрддрд╛рд░рдГ (рджреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдВ рдиреЛрджреНрдпрдореН)

рдкрд░рд╕реНрдкрд░реЛрдкрдХрд╛рд░реНрдпреЛрдкрдХрд╛рд░рдХ-рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рджрд┐рд╖реНрд╡реН рдЗрд╡рд╛рддреНрд░рд╛рдкрд┐ рди рд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзрдГ ред

English

The answer is as follows:-
There is nothing inconsistent in this,
as it is possible for the same person to render help to another
and also to receive help from him.

Espa├▒ol

La respuesta es la siguiente:-
No hay nada inconsistente en esto,
ya que es posible que la misma persona brinde ayuda a otra
y tambi├йn para recibir ayuda de ├йl.

owing to an appreciation of their qualities or character

English

By those who have done what should be done (prapannas),
who understand this subtle truth and are convinced of it,
the grace of devotees who are exclusively and supremely attached to the Lord
will be desired as an end in itself -
devotees who are free from the following stains :
the desire for transgressing the Lord’s commands,
excess of doubt,
connection with other deities,
enjoyment depending on one’s own effort
and enjoyment for one’s own self.

quienes entienden esta verdad sutil
y est├бn convencidos de ella,
La gracia de los devotos
que est├бn unidos exclusiva y supremamente al Se├▒or
ser├б deseado como un fin en s├н mismo -
devotos libres de las siguientes manchas:
el deseo de transgredir las ├│rdenes del Se├▒or,
exceso de duda,
conexi├│n con otras deidades,
disfrute dependiendo del propio esfuerzo

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ (рддре░рдкре░)

рд╡рд┐рд╕реНрддрд╛рд░рдГ (рджреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдВ рдиреЛрджреНрдпрдореН)

рд╡реЗрдж-рдЬреНрдЮ-рднрд╛рдЧрд╡рдд–рд╡рд┐рд╕реНрдордпрд╛рд╡рд╣-рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢-рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдг-рдЧреБрдгрдХреЗрди рдирд╛рдереЗрди
рд╕рдВрдХрд▓реНрдкрд┐рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдиреБрд╡рдиреНрддреЛ рд╡рдпрдВ
рддрджреАрдп-рд╕рджреН-рджрд╛рд╕рд╛рдирд╛рдореН рдЕрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд░реЗрдг рджрд╛рд╕реНрдпрдореН рдЕрднреНрдпреБрдкреЗрддреНрдп,
рдЕрд╡рд┐рдирд╢реНрд╡рд░-рд╡реЗрдж-рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░-рдиреАрддрд┐-рд╡реНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрдерд╛рдкрд┐рддрд╛ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐рд░реН рдпрдерд╛ рди рд╣реАрдпреЗрдд
рддрдерд╛ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╛рдГ рд╕реНрдордГ рее

English

We that accept the code of conduct prescribed by the Lord,
whose auspicious qualities fill, with astonishment, Bh─Бgavatas
who have understood the meaning of the Vedas -
We conduct ourselves in such a way that
we do not deviate from the righteous path ordained in the eternal Vedas
in rendering service to His good devotees with extreme reverence to them.

Espa├▒ol

Nosotros que aceptamos el C├│digo de Conducta prescrito por el Se├▒or,
cuyas cualidades auspiciosas se llenan, con asombro, bh─Бgavatas
quienes han entendido el significado de los Vedas -
Nos llevamos a nosotros mismos de tal manera que
No nos desviamos del camino justo ordenado en los vedas eternos
al prestar servicio a sus buenos devotos con extrema reverencia hacia ellos.

English

With our words which emit a fragrance
that would be eagerly desired by the lotus
which arose in the pond of the Lord’s navel,
we do not beg of the Lord the pleasures of this world and of svarga which are like straw
nor kaivalya nor even mokс╣гa .
We only pray that we should have the grace of the pure and firm-minded Bh─Бgavatas,
who are like the chaste wives in the royal harem,
for their grace is like the dawn
which heralds the day of the splendour of mokс╣гa.

Espa├▒ol

Con nuestras palabras que emiten una fragancia
que ser├нa deseado ansiosamente por el loto
que surgi├│ en el estanque del ombligo del Se├▒or,
No le suplicamos al Se├▒or los placeres de este mundo y de Svarga que son como la paja
ni kaivalya ni incluso mokс╣гa.
Solo rezamos para que tengamos la gracia de los Bh─Бgavatas puros y de mente firme,
quienes son como las esposas castas en el har├йn real,
Porque su gracia es como el amanecer
que anuncia el d├нa del esplendor de Mokс╣гa.
